[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Memory corruption: double-free. A region freed once in `static_destruct` is freed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magain later in `parse_path_argument`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The first free happens in the teardown section of the fuzzer harness [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`static_destruct` in `fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The second free originates from `parse_path_argument` in [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/shared/parse-argument.c` after a call to [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`path_extend_internal` in `path-util.c`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer backtrace clearly shows the Allocate→Free→Free sequence on the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame pointer.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Relevant Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `src/shared/parse-argument.c` → `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m in the build [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `src/basic/path-util.c` → `path_extend_internal` and `path_make_absolute_cwd` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mrealloc and buffer handling[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. `src/basic/static-destruct.h` → teardown logic invoked by the fuzz harness  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Fuzzer entry point `src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c` to understand [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe lifecycle of allocated resources  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Holistic View  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To fully understand how the double-free arises, one should trace the allocation [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand ownership of the buffer from its creation or reallocation in `path-util.c`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough its consumption in `parse_path_argument`, to its cleanup in the harness’s [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic destruct routines. A review of reference counting or ownership transfer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconventions in the surrounding API will clarify why the buffer is freed twice.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
